2 Sec. LLLLL-1. 34-B MRSA §5003-B is enacted to read 
3 §5003-B. Services across the lifespan 
4 The department shall facilitate the development of a home and commumty-based 
5 waiver from the Umted States Department of Health and Human Services, Centers for 
6 Medicare and Medicaid Services that provides services for persons with mtellectual and 
7 developmental disabilities, autism or other related conditions across the lifespan, mcludmg 
8 smooth transit10ns from childhood to adulthood Upon federal approval, the department 
9 shall adopt rules to implement this sect10n Rules adopted pursuant to this section are maJ or 
10 substantive rules as defined m Title 5, chapter 375, subchapter 2-A, except that any 
11 subsequent amendments to those rules are routme techmcal rules as defined m Title 5, 
12 chapter 375, subchapter 2-A 
13 Sec. LLLLL-2. Home and community-based lifespan program. The 
14 Department of Health and Human Services shall establish a MameCare home and 
15 commumty-based lifespan program for md1V1duals with mtellectual and developmental 
16 disabilities, autism or other related condit10ns pursuant to the Mame Revised Statutes, Title 
17 34-B, sect10n 5003-B, referred to m this Part as "the lifespan program " On or after Apnl 
18 1, 2025, the department may begm enrollment m the lifespan program The department 
19 may seek waivers or other approvals from the federal Department of Health and Human 
20 Services, Centers for Medicare and Medicaid Services to implement the lifespan program 
21 The goals of the lifespan program are to 
22 1. Flexibility across the bfespan. Provide home and commumty-based supports that 
23 can change over the member's lifespan as a member as descnbed m this section and the 
24 persons who provide support to that member get older, without needmg to move from one 
25 waiver program to another, 
26 2. Seamless transitions. Expand upon the department's current childhood-to-
